  - Dimethylformamide (CAS: 68-12-2)
  - Water (CAS: 7732-18-5)

**Reaction Conditions:**
  - Time: 18.25 hours
  - Yield: 99%

**SMILES:**
  - Reactants: `CN(/N=C/c1cccc(Cl)c1F)C(=O)[C@@H](NC(=O)OC(C)(C)C)C1CCCCC1.CC(C)(C)OC(=O)N[C@H](C(=O)O)C(C)(C)C`
  - Products: `CN(/N=C/c1cccc(Cl)c1F)C(=O)[C@@H](NC(=O)[C@@H](NC(=O)OC(C)(C)C)C(C)(C)C)C1CCCCC1`
